Literature review is concept centric?

Select one:
True
False
ChatGPT
True

A literature review is typically concept-centric, as it focuses on summarizing and analyzing the key concepts, theories, and findings relevant to a particular research topic or question. It aims to provide an overview of the existing literature, emphasizing the concepts and ideas presented in the reviewed works.
